3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (3 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input class="input w-input" data-name="Footer Subscribe 2" id="Footer-Subscribe-2" maxlength="256" name="Footer-Subscribe-2" placeholder="Email address" required="" type="email"/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input class="search-form-input w-input" id="search" maxlength="256" name="query" placeholder="Søk..." required="" type="search"/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

2.4.1 Hopp over blokker (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.1 (2.4.1 - Nivå A)

Add aria-label or aria-labelledby attribute
